        points: {
            totalAwarded: number;
            totalEntries: number;
            avgPerEntry: number;
        };
        submissions: {
            total: number;
            pending: number;
            approved: number;
            rejected: number;
            approvalRate: number;
        };
        users: {
            total: number;
            active: number;
            withSubmissions: number;
            withBadges: number;
            activationRate: number;
        };
        badges: {
            totalBadges: number;
            totalEarned: number;
            uniqueEarners: number;
        };
        reviews: {
            pendingReviews: number;
            avgReviewTimeHours: number;
        };
    };
    distributions: {
        submissionsByStatus: {
            status: string;
            count: number;
        }[];
        submissionsByActivity: {
            activity: string;
            count: number;
            activityName?: string | undefined;
        }[];
        usersByRole: {
            role: string;
            count: number;
        }[];
        pointsByActivity: {
            entries: number;
            activity: string;
            totalPoints: number;
            activityName?: string | undefined;
        }[];
        usersByCohort?: {
            cohort: string | null;
            count: number;
        }[] | undefined;
        pointsDistribution?: {
            totalUsers: number;
            max: number;
            min: number;
            avg: number;
            percentiles: {
                value: number;
                percentile: number;
            }[];
        } | undefined;
    };
    trends: {
        submissionsByDate: {
            date: string;
            total: number;
            pending: number;
            approved: number;
            rejected: number;
        }[];
        userRegistrationsByDate: {
            date: string;
            count: number;
        }[];
    };
    recentActivity: {
        submissions: {
            status: string;
            created_at: string;
            activity: {
                name: string;
            };
            user: {

                handle: string;
            };
            id: string;
        }[];

            email: string;

            role: string;
            id: string;
        }[];

                name: string;
            };

                handle: string;
            };
            id: string;
            updated_at: string;
        }[];
    };
    performance: {
        reviewers: {
            total: number;
            name: string;
            handle: string;
            role: string;
            id: string;
            approved: number;
            rejected: number;
        }[];
        topBadges: {
            badge: {
                code?: string | undefined;
                name?: string | undefined;
                icon_url?: string | null | undefined;

                [k: string]: unknown;
            };

        }[];

}>;

export type AdminSubmissionsQuery = z.infer<typeof AdminSubmissionsQuerySchema>;

// @public (undocumented)
export const AdminSubmissionsQuerySchema: z.ZodObject<{
    status: z.ZodDefault<z.ZodEnum<["ALL", "PENDING", "APPROVED", "REJECTED", "REVOKED"]>>;
    activity: z.ZodDefault<z.ZodEnum<["ALL", "LEARN", "EXPLORE", "AMPLIFY", "PRESENT", "SHINE"]>>;
    userId: z.ZodOptional<z.ZodString>;
    page: z.ZodDefault<z.ZodNumber>;
    limit: z.ZodDefault<z.ZodNumber>;
    sortBy: z.ZodDefault<z.ZodEnum<["created_at", "updated_at", "status"]>>;
    sortOrder: z.ZodDefault<z.ZodEnum<["asc", "desc"]>>;
}, "strip", z.ZodTypeAny, {
    page: number;

// @public (undocumented)
export class APIError extends ElevateApiError {
    constructor(message: string, status: number, details?: unknown[] | undefined);
    // (undocumented)
    details?: unknown[] | undefined;
    // (undocumented)
    status: number;
}

// @public (undocumented)
export interface ApiError {
    // (undocumented)
    code?: string;
    // (undocumented)
    details?: unknown;
    // (undocumented)
    error: string;
    // (undocumented)
    success: false;
    // (undocumented)
    timestamp?: string;
    // (undocumented)
    traceId?: string;
}

// @public (undocumented)
export class ElevateApiError extends Error {
    constructor(message: string, code?: ErrorCode, details?: unknown, traceId?: string);
    // (undocumented)
    readonly code: ErrorCode;
    // (undocumented)
    readonly details?: unknown;
    // (undocumented)
    readonly severity: ErrorSeverityLevel;
    // (undocumented)
    readonly statusCode: number;
    // (undocumented)
    readonly traceId?: string;
}

// @public (undocumented)
export interface ErrorEnvelope {
    // (undocumented)
    code: string;
    // (undocumented)
    details?: Record<string, unknown>;
    // (undocumented)
    message: string;
    // (undocumented)
    type: ErrorEnvelopeType;
}

// @public (undocumented)
export type ErrorEnvelopeType = 'validation' | 'cap' | 'state' | 'auth' | 'idempotency';

// @public (undocumented)
export const ErrorSeverity: {
    readonly LOW: "low";
    readonly MEDIUM: "medium";
    readonly HIGH: "high";
    readonly CRITICAL: "critical";
};

// @public (undocumented)
export type ErrorSeverityLevel = (typeof ErrorSeverity)[keyof typeof ErrorSeverity];

// @public (undocumented)
export const ErrorSeverityMap: Record<ErrorCode, ErrorSeverityLevel>;

// @public (undocumented)
export const ErrorStatusCodes: Record<ErrorCode, number>;

        id: string;
        activity_code: string;

            name: string;
            code: string;
        };
        status: string;
        visibility: string;
        payload: Record<string, unknown>;

        updated_at: Date | string;

}): UserProfileDTO;

// @public (undocumented)
export interface PaginatedAnalytics<T> {
    // (undocumented)
    data: T[];
    // (undocumented)
    filters: AnalyticsFilters;
    // (undocumented)
    generatedAt: string;
    // (undocumented)
    pagination: {
        total: number;
        page: number;
        limit: number;
        totalPages: number;
    };
}

// @public (undocumented)
export type PaginatedResponse<T> = {
    data: T[];
    total: number;
    page: number;
    limit: number;
    totalPages: number;
};

// @public
export const PaginatedResponseSchema: <T extends z.ZodTypeAny>(dataSchema: T) => z.ZodObject<{
    data: z.ZodArray<T, "many">;
    total: z.ZodNumber;
    page: z.ZodNumber;
    limit: z.ZodNumber;
    totalPages: z.ZodNumber;
}, "strip", z.ZodTypeAny, {
    page: number;
    limit: number;
    data: T["_output"][];
    total: number;
    totalPages: number;
}, {
    page: number;
    limit: number;
    data: T["_input"][];
    total: number;
    totalPages: number;
}>;

// @public (undocumented)
export interface PaginationConfig {
    // (undocumented)
    limit: number;
    // (undocumented)
    onPageChange: (page: number) => void;
    // (undocumented)
    page: number;
    // (undocumented)
    pages?: number;
    // (undocumented)
    total: number;
}

// @public (undocumented)
export type PaginationParams = z.infer<typeof PaginationParamsSchema>;

// @public
export const PaginationParamsSchema: z.ZodObject<{
    page: z.ZodDefault<z.ZodNumber>;
    limit: z.ZodDefault<z.ZodNumber>;
    offset: z.ZodOptional<z.ZodNumber>;
}, "strip", z.ZodTypeAny, {
    page: number;
    limit: number;
    offset?: number | undefined;
}, {
    offset?: number | undefined;
    page?: number | undefined;
    limit?: number | undefined;
}>;

// @public (undocumented)

}, "strip", z.ZodTypeAny, {

    submissions: z.ZodArray<z.ZodObject<{
        id: z.ZodString;
        activity_code: z.ZodEnum<["LEARN", "EXPLORE", "AMPLIFY", "PRESENT", "SHINE"]>;
        user_name: z.ZodString;
        created_at: z.ZodString;
        status: z.ZodEnum<["PENDING", "APPROVED", "REJECTED", "REVOKED"]>;
    }, "strip", z.ZodTypeAny, {
        status: "PENDING" | "APPROVED" | "REJECTED" | "REVOKED";

        status: "PENDING" | "APPROVED" | "REJECTED" | "REVOKED";

        created_at: string;

        user_name: string;
    }>, "many">;
    approvals: z.ZodArray<z.ZodObject<{
        id: z.ZodString;
        activity_code: z.ZodEnum<["LEARN", "EXPLORE", "AMPLIFY", "PRESENT", "SHINE"]>;

        user_name: string;
        reviewer_name: string;
        approved_at: string;
    }>, "many">;
    users: z.ZodArray<z.ZodObject<{
        id: z.ZodString;
        name: z.ZodString;
        created_at: z.ZodString;
        cohort: z.ZodNullable<z.ZodString>;

        name: string;
        id: string;

        created_at: string;

// @public (undocumented)
export class ReferralError extends ElevateApiError {
    constructor(code: 'SELF_REFERRAL' | 'CIRCULAR_REFERRAL', details?: unknown, traceId?: string);
}

// @public (undocumented)

}, "strip", z.ZodTypeAny, {

    email: string;
    activityName: string;
    reviewerNote: string;
    dashboardUrl: string;
    supportUrl: string;
}, {
    name: string;
    email: string;
    activityName: string;
    reviewerNote: string;

    supportUrl: string;
}>;

// @public (undocumented)
export const RemoveBadgeSchema: z.ZodObject<{
    badgeCode: z.ZodString;
    userIds: z.ZodArray<z.ZodString, "many">;
    reason: z.ZodOptional<z.ZodString>;
}, "strip", z.ZodTypeAny, {
    userIds: string[];
    badgeCode: string;
    reason?: string | undefined;
}, {
    userIds: string[];
    badgeCode: string;
    reason?: string | undefined;
}>;

// @public (undocumented)
export const ReviewSubmissionSchema: z.ZodObject<{
    submissionId: z.ZodString;
    action: z.ZodEnum<["approve", "reject"]>;
    reviewNote: z.ZodOptional<z.ZodString>;
    pointAdjustment: z.ZodOptional<z.ZodNumber>;
}, "strip", z.ZodTypeAny, {
    submissionId: string;
    action: "approve" | "reject";
    reviewNote?: string | undefined;
    pointAdjustment?: number | undefined;
}, {
    submissionId: string;
    action: "approve" | "reject";
    reviewNote?: string | undefined;
    pointAdjustment?: number | undefined;
}>;

// @public
export type Role = UserRole;

// @public
export const ROLE_FILTER_OPTIONS: readonly ["ALL", "PARTICIPANT", "REVIEWER", "ADMIN", "SUPERADMIN"];

// @public (undocumented)
export const RoleEnum: z.ZodEnum<["PARTICIPANT", "REVIEWER", "ADMIN", "SUPERADMIN"]>;

// @public (undocumented)
export type RoleFilterOption = typeof ROLE_FILTER_OPTIONS[number];

// @public (undocumented)
export const RoleFilterSchema: z.ZodEnum<["ALL", "PARTICIPANT", "REVIEWER", "ADMIN", "SUPERADMIN"]>;

// @public (undocumented)
export const RoleSchema: z.ZodEnum<["PARTICIPANT", "REVIEWER", "ADMIN", "SUPERADMIN"]>;

// @public (undocumented)
export type RoleType = UserRole;

// @public (undocumented)
export interface SafeBadge {
    // (undocumented)
    code: string;
    // (undocumented)
    description?: string;
    // (undocumented)
    earned_at?: string;
    // (undocumented)
    icon_url?: string | null;
    // (undocumented)
    name: string;
}

// @public (undocumented)
export const SafeBadgeSchema: z.ZodObject<{
    code: z.ZodString;
    name: z.ZodString;
    description: z.ZodOptional<z.ZodString>;
    icon_url: z.ZodOptional<z.ZodNullable<z.ZodString>>;
    earned_at: z.ZodOptional<z.ZodString>;
}, "strip", z.ZodTypeAny, {
    code: string;
    name: string;
    description?: string | undefined;
    icon_url?: string | null | undefined;
    earned_at?: string | undefined;
}, {
    code: string;
    name: string;
    description?: string | undefined;
    icon_url?: string | null | undefined;
    earned_at?: string | undefined;
}>;

// @public (undocumented)
export interface SafeDashboardData {
    // (undocumented)
    badges: SafeBadge[];
    // (undocumented)
    points: {
        total: number;
        breakdown: Record<string, number>;
    };
    // (undocumented)
    progress: ProgressStage[];
    // (undocumented)
    recentActivity: {
        id: string;
        activityCode: string;
        activityName: string;
        status: string;
        created_at: string;
        updated_at: string;
    }[];
    // (undocumented)
    stats: DashboardStats;
    // (undocumented)
    user: SafeUser;
}

            activityCode: "EXPLORE";
        } | {
            data: {
                peers_trained: number;
                students_trained: number;
                session_date: string;
                attendance_proof_files?: string[] | undefined;
                session_start_time?: string | undefined;
                duration_minutes?: number | undefined;
                location?: {
                    venue?: string | undefined;
                    city?: string | undefined;
                    country?: string | undefined;
                } | undefined;
                session_title?: string | undefined;
                co_facilitators?: string[] | undefined;
                evidence_note?: string | undefined;
            };
            activityCode: "AMPLIFY";
        } | {
            data: {
                linkedin_url: string;
                caption: string;
                screenshot_url?: string | undefined;
            };
            activityCode: "PRESENT";
        } | {
            data: {
                idea_title: string;
                idea_summary: string;
                attachments?: string[] | undefined;
            };
            activityCode: "SHINE";
        } | null;
        hasCompleted: boolean;
    }[];
}, {
    points: {
        total: number;
        breakdown: Record<string, number>;
    };
    user: {
        name: string;
        handle: string;
        id: string;
        school?: string | null | undefined;
        email?: string | undefined;
        cohort?: string | null | undefined;
        role?: "PARTICIPANT" | "REVIEWER" | "ADMIN" | "SUPERADMIN" | undefined;
        avatar_url?: string | null | undefined;
    };
    badges: {
        code: string;
        name: string;
        description?: string | undefined;
        icon_url?: string | null | undefined;
        earned_at?: string | undefined;
    }[];
    recentActivity: {
        status: string;
        created_at: string;
        activityCode: string;
        id: string;
        updated_at: string;
        activityName: string;
    }[];
    stats: {
        totalSubmissions: number;
        approvedSubmissions: number;
        pendingSubmissions: number;
        completedStages: number;
    };
    progress: {
        activityCode: string;
        activityName: string;
        defaultPoints: number;
        pointsEarned: number;
        submissionCounts: {
            total: number;
            pending: number;
            approved: number;
            rejected: number;
        };
        latestSubmission: {
            data: {
                provider: "SPL" | "ILS";
                course_name: string;
                completed_at: string;
                certificate_url?: string | undefined;
                certificate_hash?: string | undefined;
            };
            activityCode: "LEARN";
        } | {
            data: {
                reflection: string;
                class_date: string;
                school?: string | undefined;
                evidence_files?: string[] | undefined;
            };
            activityCode: "EXPLORE";
        } | {
            data: {
                peers_trained: number;
                students_trained: number;
                session_date: string;
                attendance_proof_files?: string[] | undefined;
                session_start_time?: string | undefined;
                duration_minutes?: number | undefined;
                location?: {
                    venue?: string | undefined;
                    city?: string | undefined;
                    country?: string | undefined;
                } | undefined;
                session_title?: string | undefined;
                co_facilitators?: string[] | undefined;
                evidence_note?: string | undefined;
            };
            activityCode: "AMPLIFY";
        } | {
            data: {
                linkedin_url: string;
                caption: string;
                screenshot_url?: string | undefined;
            };
            activityCode: "PRESENT";
        } | {
            data: {
                idea_title: string;
                idea_summary: string;
                attachments?: string[] | undefined;
            };
            activityCode: "SHINE";
        } | null;
        hasCompleted: boolean;
    }[];
}>;

}

// @public (undocumented)
export const StatusFilterSchema: z.ZodEnum<["ALL", "PENDING", "APPROVED", "REJECTED", "REVOKED"]>;

// @public (undocumented)
export type StatusValue = typeof STATUS_VALUES[number];

// @public (undocumented)
export interface Submission {
    // (undocumented)
    activity_code: string;
    // (undocumented)
    created_at: Date;
    // (undocumented)
    id: string;
    // (undocumented)
    payload: unknown;
    // (undocumented)
    review_note: string | null;
    // (undocumented)
    reviewer_id: string | null;
    // (undocumented)
    status: SubmissionStatus;
    // (undocumented)
    updated_at: Date;
    // (undocumented)
    user_id: string;
    // (undocumented)
    visibility: Visibility;
}

// @public
export const SUBMISSION_STATUSES: readonly ["PENDING", "APPROVED", "REJECTED", "REVOKED"];

export const SubmissionAttachmentSchema: z.ZodObject<{

                path: string;

                name: string;

                school?: string | null | undefined;
                cohort?: string | null | undefined;

                default_points?: number | undefined;
            };

                name: string;
                id: string;
                handle: string;
                email?: string | undefined;
                school?: string | null | undefined;
                cohort?: string | null | undefined;
            } | null | undefined;
            reviewed_at?: string | null | undefined;
        };
        evidence?: string | undefined;
    };
    success: true;
}, {
    data: {
        submission: {
            status: "PENDING" | "APPROVED" | "REJECTED" | "REVOKED";

// @public (undocumented)
export interface SubmissionDTO {
    // (undocumented)
    activity: {
        name: string;
        code: string;
    };
    // (undocumented)
    activityCode: 'LEARN' | 'EXPLORE' | 'AMPLIFY' | 'PRESENT' | 'SHINE';
    // (undocumented)
    createdAt: string;
    // (undocumented)
    id: string;
    // (undocumented)
    payload: Record<string, unknown>;
    // (undocumented)
    status: 'PENDING' | 'APPROVED' | 'REJECTED' | 'REVOKED';
    // (undocumented)
    updatedAt: string;
    // (undocumented)
    visibility: 'PUBLIC' | 'PRIVATE';
}

    updatedAt: z.ZodString;
}, "strip", z.ZodTypeAny, {

    };

    createdAt: string;
    updatedAt: string;

}, "strip", z.ZodTypeAny, {

// @public (undocumented)
export const TrendAnalysisSchema: z.ZodObject<{
    period: z.ZodEnum<["7d", "30d", "90d"]>;
    metric: z.ZodEnum<["submissions", "points", "users", "approvals"]>;
    data: z.ZodArray<z.ZodObject<{
        date: z.ZodString;
        value: z.ZodNumber;
        label: z.ZodOptional<z.ZodString>;
    }, "strip", z.ZodTypeAny, {
        value: number;
        date: string;
        label?: string | undefined;
    }, {
        value: number;
        date: string;
        label?: string | undefined;
    }>, "many">;
    summary: z.ZodObject<{
        total: z.ZodNumber;
        average: z.ZodNumber;
        growth: z.ZodNumber;
        trend: z.ZodEnum<["up", "down", "stable"]>;
    }, "strip", z.ZodTypeAny, {
        total: number;
        average: number;
        growth: number;
        trend: "up" | "down" | "stable";
    }, {
        total: number;
        average: number;
        growth: number;
        trend: "up" | "down" | "stable";
    }>;
}, "strip", z.ZodTypeAny, {
    data: {
        value: number;
        date: string;
        label?: string | undefined;
